Let Chaos Reign
Ongoing Scheme

None May Outshine Me
Scheme
When you set this scheme in motion, choose one—
• Each opponent who controls more permanents than you sacrifices permanents equal to the difference.
• Each opponent who has more cards in hand than you discards cards equal to the difference.
• Each opponent who has more life than you loses life equal to the difference.
"Spite has gotten me this far. I see no reason to stop now."
That Nuisance Never Was
Scheme
When you set this scheme in motion, exile target nonbasic permanent you don't control. Search your opponents' graveyards, hands, and libraries for all cards with the same name as that permanent and exile them. Then those players shuffle their libraries.
"I do hope you weren't using that."
Your Beliefs Are Empty
Scheme
When you set this scheme in motion, each player discards all the cards from his or her hand. Then you draw cards equal to the greatest number of cards a player discarded this way and each other player draws cards equal to the lowest such number.
